"vs_2_0
def c20, 1, 0.5, 0, 0
dcl_position v0
dcl_normal v1
dcl_texcoord v2
mad oT0.xy, v2, c19, c19.zwzw
dp4 oT2.x, c4, v0
dp4 oT2.y, c5, v0
dp4 oT2.z, c6, v0
mul r0.xyz, v1.y, c8
mad r0.xyz, c7, v1.x, r0
mad r0.xyz, c9, v1.z, r0
nrm r1.xyz, r0
mul r0.x, r1.y, r1.y

mul r2, r1.yzzx, r1.xyzz
dp4 r3.x, c15, r2
dp4 r3.y, c16, r2
dp4 r3.z, c17, r2
mad r0.xyz, c18, r0.x, r3
mov r1.w, c20.x
dp4 r2.x, c12, r1
dp4 r2.y, c13, r1
dp4 r2.z, c14, r1
mov oT1.xyz, r1
add oT3.xyz, r0, r2
dp4 r0.y, c1, v0
mul r1.x, r0.y, c10.x
mul r1.w, r1.x, c20.y
dp4 r0.x, c0, v0
dp4 r0.w, c3, v0
mul r1.xz, r0.xyww, c20.y
mad oT4.xy, r1.z, c11.zwzw, r1.xwzw
dp4 r0.z, c2, v0
mov oPos, r0
mov oT4.zw, r0

"

mad r0.x, r1.x, r1.x, -r0.x
mul r2, r1.yzzx, r1.xyzz
dp4 r3.x, c21, r2
dp4 r3.y, c22, r2
dp4 r3.z, c23, r2
mad r0.xyz, c24, r0.x, r3
mov r1.w, c26.x
dp4 r2.x, c18, r1
dp4 r2.y, c19, r1
dp4 r2.z, c20, r1
add r0.xyz, r0, r2
dp4 r2.y, c9, v0
add r3, -r2.y, c15
mul r4, r1.y, r3
mul r3, r3, r3
dp4 r2.x, c8, v0
add r5, -r2.x, c14
mad r4, r5, r1.x, r4
mad r3, r5, r5, r3
dp4 r2.z, c10, v0
add r5, -r2.z, c16
mov oT2.xyz, r2
mad r2, r5, r1.z, r4
mov oT1.xyz, r1
mad r1, r5, r5, r3
rsq r3.x, r1.x
rsq r3.y, r1.y
rsq r3.z, r1.z
rsq r3.w, r1.w
mov r4.x, c26.x
mad r1, r1, c17, r4.x
mul r2, r2, r3
max r2, r2, c26.y
rcp r3.x, r1.x
rcp r3.y, r1.y
rcp r3.z, r1.z
rcp r3.w, r1.w
mul r1, r2, r3
mul r2.xyz, r1.y, c1
mad r2.xyz, c0, r1.x, r2
mad r1.xyz, c2, r1.z, r2
mad r1.xyz, c3, r1.w, r1
add oT3.xyz, r0, r1

"
